        // Custom CLS metric.  Source: https://web.dev/cls/
        try { // Use try for 'layout-shift'
          cls = 0;
          metric = 'layout-shift';
          observer = new PerformanceObserver(function (list) {
            entries = list.getEntries();
            for (var i=0; i < entries.length; i++){
              entry = entries[i];
              if (!entry.hadRecentInput) {
                cls += entry.value;
              }
            }
            newrelic.setCustomAttribute(metric, cls); //send to NR after adding up the CLS values
          });
          observer.observe({type: 'layout-shift', buffered: true});
        } catch (e) {
          // Do nothing, if it is not supported
          console.log('NR Custom Metric', 'Unable to observe CLS/Layout Shift on this browser.');
          console.log('NR Custom Metric', 'Error:', e);
        }

      }

(function () { 
  if ( typeof window.CustomEvent === "function" ) return false;
  function CustomEvent ( event, params ) {
    params = params || { bubbles: false, cancelable: false, detail: undefined };
    var evt = document.createEvent( 'CustomEvent' );
    evt.initCustomEvent( event, params.bubbles, params.cancelable, params.detail );
    return evt;
   }
  CustomEvent.prototype = window.Event.prototype;
  window.CustomEvent = CustomEvent;
})();
var SNILoadEvents = {
  listen: function(names) {
    var evtObj = SNILoadEvents.events = {};
    for (var i=0; i < names.length; i++) {
      var name = 'SNILoadEvent_' + names[i];
      if (window.CustomEvent) {
        evtObj[names[i]] = new CustomEvent(name);
      } else {
        evtObj[names[i]] = document.createEvent('CustomEvent');
        evtObj[names[i]].initCustomEvent(name, true, true);
      }
    }
  },
  trigger: function(names) {
    var names = (typeof names === 'string') ? [ names ] : names;
    for (var i=0; i < names.length; i++) {
      try {
        window.dispatchEvent(window.SNILoadEvents.events[names[i]]);
        window.removeEventListener('SNILoadEvent_' + names[i], window.SNILoadEvents.events[names[i]].function);
        window.SNILoadEvents.events[names[i]] = { firedAlready: true };
      } catch(e) {
        if (window.console) {
          console.warn('SNILoadEvents event "' + names[i] + '" already triggered.');
        }
      }
    }
  },
  mdmLoaded: function(fn) {
    SNILoadEvents.on('mdm', function(e) {
      if (window.MetaDataManager !== 'undefined') {
        fn();
      } else {
        if (window.console) {
          console.error('MetaDataManager is not defined!');
        }
      }
    });
  },
  on: function(name, fn) {
    if (window.SNILoadEvents.events[name].firedAlready) {
      fn();
    } else {
      window.SNILoadEvents.events[name].function = fn;
      window.addEventListener('SNILoadEvent_' + name, fn);
    }
  }
};

SNILoadEvents.listen([
  'sni-all',
  'core',
  'mdm',
  'ads',
  'analytics'
]);

(function() {
  var jqMethods = 'css|hide|addClass|removeClass|find|remove|html|height|offset|animate|closest|appendTo|insertAfter|load|attr|append|on'.split('|');
  function makePlugin(parent, name, operand) {
    return function() {
      var params = arguments;
      SNILoadEvents.on('core', function() {
        var $el = window.$.apply(window.$.fn, operand);
        $el[name].apply($el, params);
      });
      return parent;
    };
  }
  window.updateJqMethods = function (name) {
    jqMethods.push(name);
  };
  window.jQuery = window.$ = function() {
    var operand = arguments;
    if (typeof arguments[0] === 'function') {
      SNILoadEvents.on('core', function() {
        window.$.apply(window.$.fn, operand);
      });
    }
    var jqMethodsObj = {};
    for (var i=0; i < jqMethods.length; i++) {
      jqMethodsObj[jqMethods[i]] = makePlugin(jqMethodsObj, jqMethods[i], operand);
    }
    return jqMethodsObj;
  };
})();

  <section class="o-Method" data-module="recipe-method" data-read-more-target="" id="mod-recipe-method-1">

    

    
    <div class="o-Method__m-Body">

      
      
        
        
         
        <ol>
          
          
            <li class="o-Method__m-Step">
              Make the ice cream cake: Brush a 3-quart metal bowl with vegetable oil; line with plastic wrap. Fill the bowl with scoops of the sorbet, vanilla ice cream and half of the chocolate ice cream, alternating small and large scoops to create a mosaic of colors and shapes. Place a piece of plastic wrap on top of the ice cream; press down to close the gaps between scoops and even out the surface. Remove the plastic wrap, sprinkle the ice cream with the wafer crumbs and re-cover with the plastic wrap, pressing gently. Freeze until set, about 30 minutes.&nbsp;
            </li>
          
            <li class="o-Method__m-Step">
              Remove the wrap and spread the remaining chocolate ice cream in an even layer on top of the crumbs. Cut the pound cake into 1/2-inch-thick slices; completely cover the ice cream with the slices, trimming as needed (you'll use about two-thirds of the cake). Cover with fresh plastic wrap and freeze until firm, at least 2 hours or up to 2 days.&nbsp;
            </li>
          
            <li class="o-Method__m-Step">
              Make the meringue: Whip the egg whites and cream of tartar in a large bowl with a mixer on medium-high speed until foamy, about 2 minutes. Gradually beat in the sugar on high speed until the whites are glossy and hold stiff peaks.&nbsp;
            </li>
          
            <li class="o-Method__m-Step">
              Remove the top layer of plastic wrap, then invert the cake onto a parchment-lined baking sheet. (If necessary, let the cake stand overturned until it slips out.) Remove the rest of the plastic wrap and cover the ice cream completely with the meringue, making the dome-shaped top slightly thicker than the sides. Form swirly peaks in the meringue using the back of a spoon. Freeze for at least 3 more hours.&nbsp;
            </li>
          
            <li class="o-Method__m-Step">
              Preheat the oven to 500 degrees. Bake the cake until the meringue peaks are golden, about 4 minutes, or brown the meringue with a blowtorch. Let the cake soften at room temperature for 5 to 10 minutes before slicing. Freeze any leftovers.&nbsp;
            </li>
          
        </ol>
      



    </div>
  </section>

        orig_date,

      try {
        if (opd && typeof opd === 'string') {
          opd_array = opd.match(/\d\d\d\d-\d\d-\d\d/g)
          opd_string = opd_array ? opd_array.join('|') : ''
          if (opd_string !== '') {
            if (opd_array[0]) {
              orig_date = new Date(opd_array[0])
              opd_string += '|' + dateDeltas(orig_date)
            }
            if (opd_array[1]) {
              mod_date = new Date(opd_array[1])
              opd_string += '|' + dateDeltas(mod_date)
            }
          }
        }
      } catch (e) {
        //  something went wrong
      }
      return opd_string
    }
    dateDeltas = function s_dateDeltas (dateObj) {
      var today = new Date(),
        days = Math.floor(
          Math.abs(today.getTime() - dateObj.getTime()) / (1000 * 3600 * 24)
        )
      if (days < 8) {
        return days + (days === 1 ? ' day' : ' days')
      } else if (days > 7 && days < 31) {
        return '8 days-1 month'
      } else if (days > 30 && days < 366) {
        return (
          Math.floor(days / 30.417) + '-' + Math.ceil(days / 30.417) + ' months'
        )
      } else if (days > 365) {
        return '>1 year'
      }
    }

    // refresh context data
    var key, value, upperKey
    for (key in mdManager.getKeys()) {
      value = mdManager.getParameter(key)
      upperKey = key.toString().toUpperCase()
      if (upperKey !== 'UNIQUEID') {
        value = value.toString().toLowerCase()
      }

      // remap mdManager to appropriate contextData variables
      if (upperKey === 'URL') {
        key = 'pageName'
      } else if (upperKey === 'TITLE') {
        key = 'pageTitle'
      } else if (upperKey === 'CATEGORYDSPNAME') {
        key = 'contentSiteSection'
      } else if (upperKey === 'SCTNDSPNAME') {
        key = 'contentSubSection'
      } else if (upperKey === 'SUBSECTION') {
        key = 'contentSubSection2'
      } else if (upperKey === 'SUBSECTIONL2') {
        key = 'contentSubSection3'
      } // verify key is correct format and if this is being used at all
      else if (upperKey === 'TYPE') {
        key = 'contentPageType'
      } else if (upperKey === 'UNIQUEID') {
        key = 'pageUniqueID'
      } else if (upperKey === 'DELIVERY_CHANNEL') {
        key = 'deliveryChannel'
      } else if (upperKey === 'IMGURL') {
        key = 'imageURL'
      } else if (upperKey === 'ORIGPUBDATE') {
        s.contextData['originalPublishDate'] = mdManager
          .getParameter(key)
          .split('|')[0]
        s.contextData['latestPublishDate'] = mdManager
          .getParameter(key)
          .split('|')[1]
        value = cleanOrigPubDate()
      } else if (upperKey === 'SHOW_ABBR') {
        key = 'showName'
      } else if (upperKey === 'POINTOFINTEREST') {
        key = 'poi'
      } else if (upperKey === 'FILTER') {
        key = 'searchFilters'
      } else if (upperKey === 'SEARCHTERMS') {
        key = 'searchTermContextual'
      } else if (upperKey === 'DIMENSIONS') {
        key = 'searchDimensions'
      } else if (upperKey === 'DIMENSIONVALUES') {
        key = 'searchDimensionValues'
      } else if (upperKey === 'NOSEARCHRESULTS') {
        key = 'noResultsSearchTerm'
      } else if (upperKey === 'TAGGROUP1') {
        key = 'contentTags'
      }

      delete s.contextData[key]
      s.contextData[key] = value
    }

    //** adding platform logic
    s.contextData.platform = 'web'

    /** content tags and s.products **/
    // clear values from previous clicks e.g. so data doesn't persist on slides that don't have products
    var usingShopTrack =
      sessionStorage.getItem('prodSetByShopTrack') != 'true' ? false : true
    if (s.events && !usingShopTrack) {
      s.events = s.events.replace(/,?prodView/, '')
    }
    if (s.linkTrackVars && !usingShopTrack) {
      // don't clear out these values if using shopTrack() function
      s.linkTrackVars = s.linkTrackVars.replace(/,?shoppingProducts/, '')
      s.linkTrackVars = s.linkTrackVars.replace(
        /,?eventShoppingProductsImpressions/,
        ''
      )
    }
    // set values
    setContentTagsFromHeaders = function conTagFromH (tagHeaders) {
      if (!Array.isArray(tagHeaders)) {
        return false
      }
      s.contextData['contentTags'] = ''
      var tagArray = []
      for (var i = 0; i < tagHeaders.length; i++) {
        var currentHeader = tagHeaders[i]
        var tagItem = currentHeader + '|'
        if (mdManager.getParameter(currentHeader) != undefined) {
          tagItem += mdManager.getParameter(currentHeader)
        }
        tagArray.push(tagItem)
      }
      s.contextData['contentTags'] = tagArray.join().toLowerCase()
    }
    var tagHeaders = [],
      lowerCaseType
    var fullURL = location.href
    var domainRegex = /^https?\:\/\/(?:.*\.)?(?:([^\.]+)\.com).*$/
    var domain = fullURL.match(domainRegex)[1]
    lowerCaseType = mdManager.getParameter('type').toString().toLowerCase()
    // collect tags and s.products under certain conditions
    if (
      lowerCaseType === 'recipe' &&
      (domain === 'foodnetwork' || domain === 'cookingchanneltv')
    ) {
      tagHeaders = [
        'cuisine',
        'difficulty',
        'mainingredient',
        'mealpart',
        'preptime',
        'technique',
        'dish',
        'mealtype',
        'nutrition',
        'occasions',
        'courses',
        'taste'
      ]
      setContentTagsFromHeaders(tagHeaders)
    } else if (
      lowerCaseType === 'example_other_page_type' &&
      domain === 'someParticularSite'
    ) {
      tagHeaders = ['ex_tag_header_1', 'ex_tag_header_2']
      setContentTagsFromHeaders(tagHeaders)
    } else {
      // overwrite contentTags if any of the following are present
      if (!usingShopTrack) {
        if (mdManager.getParameterString('Overlay_TagGroup1') != '') {
          s.contextData['contentTags'] = mdManager
            .getParameterString('Overlay_TagGroup1')
            .replace(/;/g, '|')
        } else if (mdManager.getParameterString('TagGroup1') != '') {
          s.contextData['contentTags'] = mdManager
            .getParameterString('TagGroup1')
            .replace(/;/g, '|')
        }
        // remove legacy wayfair stl from the photo tags/list2 meta-data
        if (
          s.contextData['contentTags'] &&
          s.contextData['contentTags'].indexOf('wayfair/shop_this_look') != -1
        ) {
          s.contextData['contentTags'] = s.contextData['contentTags'].replace(
            'partner|wayfair/shop_this_look,',
            ''
          )
        }
        if (
          mdManager.getParameterString('shopping').toString().toLowerCase() ==
          'shopping'
        ) {
          if (mdManager.getParameter('products').indexOf('|') == -1) {
            productList = mdManager
              .getParameter('products')
              .replace(/,;/g, ',;s|na|')
            s.products = ';s|na|' + productList
          } else {
            productList = mdManager
              .getParameter('products')
              .replace(/,;/g, ',;s|')
            s.products = ';s|' + productList
          }
          s.products += ',;c|' + mdManager.getParameter('componentName')
          s.products += '|' + mdManager.getParameter('componentTitle')
          s.products += '|' + mdManager.getParameter('imageCount')
          s.products += '|' + mdManager.getParameter('productCount')
          s.products += '|' + mdManager.getParameter('visibleProductCount')
          s.products += '|' + mdManager.getParameter('perImageProductCount')
          s.products += '|' + mdManager.getParameter('productPosition')

          s.products = s.products.toLowerCase()
          s.contextData['shoppingProducts'] = 'D=products'
          s.contextData['eventShoppingProductsImpressions'] = '1'
          s.linkTrackVars = s.linkTrackVars || ''
          s.linkTrackVars +=
            ',shoppingProducts,eventShoppingProductsImpressions'
          s.events = s.events || ''
          s.events += ',prodView'

          //For Apple News shopping product clicks
          if (
            location.host.indexOf('click.tinysharks.') != -1 ||
            location.host.indexOf('click.home.') != -1 ||
            location.host.indexOf('click.fnr.') != -1
          ) {
            s.events = 'scAdd'
            s.contextData['eventShoppingProductsImpressions'] = ''
            s.contextData['moduleName'] =
              mdManager.getParameter('componentName')
            s.contextData['linkTitle'] =
              mdManager.getParameter('sourcePageTitle')
            s.contextData['linkPosition'] = 'apple news'
            s.contextData['targetURL'] = location.host + location.pathname
            s.contextData['locURL'] = mdManager.getParameter('sourcePageUrl')
          }
        }
        sessionStorage.setItem('prodSetByShopTrack', 'false') // just make sure we're still not using shopTrack()
      }
    }

    // allow a callback
    if (typeof callback === 'function') {
      callback(e, t, extra1, extra2, extra3)
    }
  }

  // modify s.t
  _satellite.logger.info('Updating s.t() to include required context data.')
  var tempTrack = s.t.bind({})
  s.t = function (e, t, extra1, extra2, extra3) {
    if (
      document.location.href.indexOf('single-video-page.embed.html') > -1 ||
      document.location.href.indexOf('/content/products/') > -1
    ) {
      _satellite.logger.warn(
        's.t() has been disabled on sites containing part of this path.'
      )
      return
    }
    // Code to run before old s.t() call
    s.contextData['eventPageConsumption'] = '1'
    s.contextData.serverCallType = 'pageview'
    s.contextData.platform = 'web'
    try {
      var thirdpartytag = 'false'

      if (
        !!_satellite.getVar('optanonconsent') &&
        _satellite.getVar('optanonconsent').indexOf('C0004:0') > -1
      ) {
        thirdpartytag = 'true'
      }
      // adding privacy logic
      s.contextData['opt.dmp'] = 'Y'
      s.contextData['opt.sell'] = 'Y'
      s.contextData['cm.ssf'] = ''
      if (thirdpartytag === 'true') {
        s.contextData['cm.ssf'] = '1'
        s.contextData['opt.dmp'] = 'N'
        s.contextData['opt.sell'] = 'N'
      }

      //privacy code end
      s.contextData['businessUnit'] = 'discovery digital studios'
      if (_satellite.getVar('Core:Constant:Analytics Code Version')) {
        s.contextData['analyticsCodeVersion'] = _satellite.getVar(
          'Core:Constant:Analytics Code Version'
        )
      }
      if (_satellite.getVar('Core:Constant:Distribution Product')) {
        s.contextData['productDetails'] = _satellite.getVar(
          'Core:Constant:Distribution Product'
        )
      }
      // old s.t() call as callback to refreshing context data
      refreshContextData(e, t, extra1, extra2, extra3, tempTrack)
      // Code to run after old s.t() call
      if (thirdpartytag === 'false') {
        runThirdPartyIntegrations()
      }
    } catch (err) {}
  }

  function runThirdPartyIntegrations () {
    _satellite.logger.info('Running Third Party Integrations')
    sendComscoreBeacon()
    sendGA_newBeacon()
    addGoogleTags()
    addFloodlightStuff()
    addPostUp_js()
    sendOtherFloodlightBeacons()
    sendDoubleClickBeacon()
  }

  function sendComscoreBeacon () {
    if (s.pe !== 'lnk_o' && s.contextData['serverCallType'] === 'pageview') {
      var ns__t = new Date().getTime(),
        cur_prot = window.location.protocol.toLowerCase(),
        cur_host = window.location.host.toLowerCase(),
        cur_path = window.location.pathname.toLowerCase()

      var path = 'https://sb.scorecardresearch.com/b'
      path += '?c1=2&c2=6035648&c3=&c4=&c5=&c6='
      path += '&c7=' + cur_prot + '//' + cur_host + cur_path
      path += '&c8=' + s.contextData['pageTitle']
      path += '&c9=' + encodeURI(s.referrer)
      path += '&c15=&ns__t=' + ns__t + '&ns_c=UTF-8'

      _satellite.logger.log('sending comscore beacon')
      var tempImg = new Image()
      tempImg.src = path
    }
  }


  function sendGA_newBeacon () {
    if (!s.pe && s.contextData['pageName']) {
      if (
        location.host.indexOf('golden.') == -1 &&
        location.host.indexOf('mynewsletters.') == -1
      ) {
        if (
          location.host.indexOf('.discovery.') != -1 ||
          location.pathname.indexOf('/discovery-com/') != -1
        ) {
          _satellite.logger.log('Adding GA')
          ;(function (i, s, o, g, r, a, m) {
            i['GoogleAnalyticsObject'] = r
            ;(i[r] =
              i[r] ||
              function () {
                ;(i[r].q = i[r].q || []).push(arguments)
              }),
              (i[r].l = 1 * new Date())
            ;(a = s.createElement(o)), (m = s.getElementsByTagName(o)[0])
            a.async = 1
            a.src = g
            m.parentNode.insertBefore(a, m)
          })(
            window,
            document,
            'script',
            'https://www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js',
            'ga'
          )

          ga('create', 'UA-43824761-30', 'auto')
          ga('send', 'pageview', {
            dimension5: _satellite.getVar('Show_Name'),
            dimension6: _satellite.getVar('Page_Type'),
            dimension24: 'non authenticated visit',
            dimension27: _satellite.getVar('Site_Name'),
            dimension28: 'web',
            dimension29: 'discovery-web'
          })

        }
      }
    }
  }

  function addGoogleTags () {
    if (!s.pe && s.pageName) {
      _satellite.logger.log('Adding Google Tags')
      $.getScript('https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=AW-935057167')
      window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || []
      function gtag () {
        dataLayer.push(arguments)
      }
      gtag('js', new Date())
      gtag('config', 'AW-935057167')
    }
  }

  function addPostUp_js () {
    if (isHGTV || isFN) {
      if (!s.pe && s.pageName) {
        _satellite.logger.log('Adding PostUp/lightboxcdn js.')
        ;(function () {
          window.setTimeout(function () {
            var e = document.createElement('script')
            e.type = 'text/javascript'
            e.async = true
            e.src =
              ('https:' == document.location.protocol
                ? 'https://'
                : 'http://') +
              'www.lightboxcdn.com/vendor/b90a8cf1-793b-4cc5-b282-f863e44f81fa/lightbox_inline.js?mb=' +
              new Date().getTime()
            var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]
            s.parentNode.insertBefore(e, s)
          }, 500)
        })()
      }
    }
  }

  function sendDoubleClickBeacon () {

        if (
          mdManager.getParameterString('Type').toLowerCase() ===
            'photogallerypage' &&

            'hg_pk_room_by_room'

          ord = Math.random()
          ord = ord * 10000000000000000000
          pixel =
            '<IMG SRC="https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackimp/N5214.3192.HGTV/B21356059.224580597;dc_trk_aid=422881682;dc_trk_cid=103475023;ord=' +
            ord +
            ';dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=;tfua=?" WIDTH="1" HEIGHT="1" BORDER="0" ALT="Advertisement">'
          $(document.body).prepend(pixel)
        }
      }
    }
  }

(function(){

    // function to refresh context data
    function refreshContextData(e,t,extra1,extra2,extra3,callback) {
        _satellite.logger.log('Refreshing Context Data.');
        // OrigPubDate modification logic
        cleanOrigPubDate = function s_cleanOrigPubDate() {
            var opd = mdManager.getParameterString("OrigPubDate"),
                opd_array = [],
                opd_days = 0,
                opd_string = "",
                orig_date,
                mod_date;
            try {
                if (opd && typeof opd === "string") {
                    opd_array = opd.match(/\d\d\d\d-\d\d-\d\d/g);
                    opd_string = opd_array ? opd_array.join("|") : "";
                    if (opd_string !== "") {
                        if (opd_array[0]) {
                            orig_date = new Date(opd_array[0]);
                            opd_string += "|" + dateDeltas(orig_date);
                        }
                        if (opd_array[1]) {
                            mod_date = new Date(opd_array[1]);
                            opd_string += "|" + dateDeltas(mod_date);
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                //  something went wrong
            }
            return opd_string;
        }
        dateDeltas = function s_dateDeltas(dateObj) {
            var today = new Date(),
                days = Math.floor(Math.abs(today.getTime() - dateObj.getTime()) / (1000 * 3600 * 24));
            if (days < 8) {
                return (days + (days === 1 ? " day" : " days"));
            } else if (days > 7 && days < 31) {
                return ("8 days-1 month");
            } else if (days > 30 && days < 366) {
                return (Math.floor(days / 30.417) + "-" + Math.ceil(days / 30.417) + " months");
            } else if (days > 365) {
                return ">1 year";
            }
        }

        // refresh context data
        var key,value,upperKey;
        for (key in mdManager.getKeys()) {
            value = mdManager.getParameter(key);
            upperKey = key.toString().toUpperCase();

            // remap mdManager to appropriate contextData variables

    		else if (upperKey  === "CATEGORYDSPNAME") { key = "contentSiteSection"; }
    		else if (upperKey  === "SCTNDSPNAME") { key = "contentSubSection"; }
    		else if (upperKey  === "SUBSECTION") { key = "contentSubSection2"; }
    		else if (upperKey  === "SUBSECTIONL2") { key = "contentSubSection3"; } // verify key is correct format and if this is being used at all

            else if (upperKey  === "POINTOFINTEREST") { key="poi"; }

            else if (upperKey  === "DIMENSIONS") { key = "searchDimensions"; }
            else if (upperKey  === "DIMENSIONVALUES") { key = "searchDimensionValues"; }
            else if (upperKey  === "NOSEARCHRESULTS") { key = "noResultsSearchTerm"; }

          s.contextData['opt.dmp']='N' ;
          s.contextData['opt.sell']='N' ;
    }
     }catch(err){
       
     }

      
        /** content tags and s.products **/
        // clear values from previous clicks e.g. so data doesn't persist on slides that don't have products
        var usingShopTrack = sessionStorage.getItem("prodSetByShopTrack") != "true"? false : true;
        if (s.events && !usingShopTrack) {
            s.events = s.events.replace(/,?prodView/, "");
        }
        if (s.linkTrackVars && !usingShopTrack) { // don't clear out these values if using shopTrack() function
            s.linkTrackVars = s.linkTrackVars.replace(/,?shoppingProducts/, "");
            s.linkTrackVars = s.linkTrackVars.replace(/,?eventShoppingProductsImpressions/, "");
        }
        // set values
        setContentTagsFromHeaders = function conTagFromH (tagHeaders) {
            if ( !Array.isArray(tagHeaders) ) { return false; };
            s.contextData["contentTags"] = "";
            var tagArray = [];
            for (var i = 0; i < tagHeaders.length; i++) {
                var currentHeader = tagHeaders[i];
                var tagItem = currentHeader + "|";
                if (mdManager.getParameter(currentHeader) != undefined) { tagItem += mdManager.getParameter(currentHeader) }
                tagArray.push(tagItem);
            }
            s.contextData["contentTags"] = tagArray.join().toLowerCase();
        };
        var tagHeaders = [],lowerCaseType;

            if (!usingShopTrack) {

                }
                if (mdManager.getParameterString("shopping").toString().toLowerCase() == "shopping") {
                    if (mdManager.getParameter("products").indexOf("|") == -1) {
                        productList = mdManager.getParameter("products").replace(/,;/g, ",;s|na|");
                        s.products = ";s|na|" + productList;
                    } else {
                        productList = mdManager.getParameter("products").replace(/,;/g, ",;s|");

                    s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("visibleProductCount");
                    s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("perImageProductCount");
                    s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("productPosition");

            }	
        }

        // allow a callback
        if (typeof callback === "function") { callback(e,t,extra1,extra2,extra3); };
    }

    _satellite.logger.info("Updating s.tl() to include required context data.");

    s.tl = function(e,t,extra1,extra2,extra3) {
        _satellite.logger.log("running modified s.tl() function.")

        s.contextData.platform = 'web';
        // old s.tl() call as callback to refreshing context data
        refreshContextData(e,t,extra1,extra2,extra3,tempLinkTrack);

    }

SNI.Analytics.moduleTrackLS = function (obj, options) {
    s.contextData["brand"] = mdManager.getParameter("site"); // make sure it is set on each use
    var origVars;
    if (!options.TargetUrl) {
        options.TargetUrl = "on page interaction";
    }
    if (!options.LocUrl) {
        options.LocUrl = document.location.href;
    }
	
	
	if (SNI.Analytics.hasLocalStorage && options.TargetUrl !== "on page interaction" && options.TargetUrl !== options.LocUrl && options.TargetUrl.indexOf(document.location.hostname) !== -1 && options.TargetUrl.indexOf('mailto:') !== 0 && options.LinkTitle.indexOf('Facebook Messenger') === -1) {
    _satellite.logger.log("Saving event to local storage to fire on next page load");
    localStorage.setItem("TRACKMOD", JSON.stringify(options));
    } else {
        origVars = s.linkTrackVars;
        s.linkTrackVars = "";
        for (var key in options) {
            s.contextData[key] = options[key].toString().replace(/https?:\/\/([^.]*).*.com\/?/, "$1.../");
            s.linkTrackVars += ",contextData." + key;
            _satellite.logger.log(key.toString() + ":" + s.contextData[key], 1);
        }
        // Add custom event
        s.contextData["eventModuleLinkClick"] = "1";
        s.linkTrackVars += ",contextData.eventModuleLinkClick";
        // fire beacon
        _satellite.logger.log('Sending s.tl call from moduleTackLS.');
        s.tl(obj, 'o', options.ModuleName);
        // clear everything out
        for (var clearKey in options) {
            s.contextData[clearKey] = "";
        }
        s.contextData["eventModuleLinkClick"] = "";
        if (typeof s.events === "string") { s.events = s.events.replace(/event24,?/, ""); };
        s.linkTrackVars = origVars;
    }
};

            var currentHeader = tagHeaders[i];
            var tagItem = currentHeader + "|";
            if (mdManager.getParameter(currentHeader) != undefined) { tagItem += mdManager.getParameter(currentHeader) }
            tagArray.push(tagItem);
        }
        s.contextData["contentTags"] = tagArray.join().toLowerCase();
    };
    var tagHeaders = [],lowerCaseType;
    var fullURL = location.href;
    var domainRegex = /^https?\:\/\/(?:.*\.)?(?:([^\.]+)\.com).*$/;
    var domain = fullURL.match(domainRegex)[1];
    lowerCaseType = mdManager.getParameter("type").toString().toLowerCase();
    // collect tags and s.products under certain conditions
    if (lowerCaseType === "recipe" && (domain === "foodnetwork" || domain === "cookingchanneltv")) {
        tagHeaders = ["cuisine", "difficulty", "mainingredient", "mealpart", "preptime", "technique", "dish", "mealtype", "nutrition", "occasions", "courses", "taste"];
        setContentTagsFromHeaders(tagHeaders);
    } else if (lowerCaseType === "example_other_page_type" && domain === "someParticularSite") {
        tagHeaders = ["ex_tag_header_1", "ex_tag_header_2"];
        setContentTagsFromHeaders(tagHeaders);
    } else {
        // overwrite contentTags if any of the following are present
        if (sessionStorage.getItem("prodSetByShopTrack") != "true") {
            if (mdManager.getParameterString("Overlay_TagGroup1") != "") {
                s.contextData["contentTags"] = mdManager.getParameterString("Overlay_TagGroup1").replace(/;/g, "|");
            } else if (mdManager.getParameterString("TagGroup1") != "") {
                s.contextData["contentTags"] = mdManager.getParameterString("TagGroup1").replace(/;/g, "|");
            }
            // remove legacy wayfair stl from the photo tags/list2 meta-data
            if (s.contextData["contentTags"] && s.contextData["contentTags"].indexOf("wayfair/shop_this_look") != -1) {
                s.contextData["contentTags"] = s.contextData["contentTags"].replace("partner|wayfair/shop_this_look,", "");
            }
            if (mdManager.getParameterString("shopping").toString().toLowerCase() == "shopping") {
                if (mdManager.getParameter("products").indexOf("|") == -1) {
                    productList = mdManager.getParameter("products").replace(/,;/g, ",;s|na|");
                    s.products = ";s|na|" + productList;
                } else {
                    productList = mdManager.getParameter("products").replace(/,;/g, ",;s|");
                    s.products = ";s|" + productList;
                }
                s.products += ",;c|" + mdManager.getParameter("componentName");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("componentTitle");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("imageCount");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("productCount");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("visibleProductCount");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("perImageProductCount");
                s.products += "|" + mdManager.getParameter("productPosition");

                s.products = s.products.toLowerCase();
                s.contextData["shoppingProducts"] = "D=products";
                s.contextData["eventShoppingProductsImpressions"] = "1";
                s.events = s.apl(s.events, "prodView", ",", 2);
            
                //For Apple News shopping product clicks
                if (location.host.indexOf("click.tinysharks.") != -1 || location.host.indexOf("click.home.") != -1 || location.host.indexOf("click.fnr.") != -1) {
                    s.events = "scAdd";
                    s.contextData["eventShoppingProductsImpressions"] = "";
                    s.contextData["moduleName"] = mdManager.getParameter("componentName");
                    s.contextData["linkTitle"] = mdManager.getParameter("sourcePageTitle");
                    s.contextData["linkPosition"] = "apple news";
                    s.contextData["targetURL"] = location.host + location.pathname;
                    s.contextData["locURL"] = mdManager.getParameter("sourcePageUrl");
                }  
            }
            sessionStorage.setItem("prodSetByShopTrack", "false");
        }	
    }
}

SNI.Analytics.trackGigyaAbandonment = function(selector) {
	var $form = $(selector);
	if ( $form.length > 0 ) {
		$form.find('input').change(function () {
			SNI.Analytics.formGigyaLast = "last_elememt:"+ $(this).attr('name');
		});
		$form.find('select').change(function () {
			SNI.Analytics.formGigyaLast = "last_elememt:"+ $(this).attr('name');
		});
		$form.submit(function () {
			SNI.Analytics.blockAbandonment = true;
		});
		$(window).bind('beforeunload',function(event){
			SNI.Analytics.fireGigyaAbandonment(event);
		});
    }
};

SNI.Analytics.trackGigyaScreenSet = function(event) {
	var modulename = event.currentScreen;
	if ( modulename === "gigya-register-email-screen" ) {
		SNI.Analytics.trackGigyaAbandonment('.gigya-screen-dialog');
	}

		var $obj = $(this);
		SNI.Analytics.moduleTrackLS(this,{
				ModuleName: modulename,
				LinkTitle: $obj.attr('title'),
				LinkPosition: $('.gigya-screen-dialog div[onclick*=providerClick], a').index($obj),
				TargetUrl: $obj.attr('title') + " Auth Screen"
			});
	});
	$('.gigya-screen-dialog a').click( function() {
		var $obj = $(this);
		if ( $obj.hasClass('gigya-screen-dialog-close') && modulename === "gigya-register-email-screen" ) {
			SNI.Analytics.fireGigyaAbandonment();
		}
		SNI.Analytics.moduleTrackLS(this,{
				ModuleName: modulename,
				LinkTitle: $obj.hasClass('gigya-screen-dialog-close') ? "close" : $obj.html(),
				LinkPosition: $('.gigya-screen-dialog div[onclick*=providerClick], a').index($obj),
				TargetUrl: $obj.attr("data-switch-screen")
			});
	});
}

var shopTrack = function (obj,shopping,componentName,componentTitle,partner,products,imageCount,productCount,visibleProductCount,perImageProductCount,productPosition,eventType) {
	_satellite.logger.log('Calling shopTrack Function'); 
  
  	var shopArgs = [].slice.call(arguments);
	_satellite.logger.log(shopArgs);
  
    sessionStorage.setItem("prodSetByShopTrack", "true");  // this will prevent the analytics doplugins code from overwriting products data set in this function
	s.trackExternalLinks=false;
	s.products="";
    s.contextData["shoppingProducts"] = "";
    // create products string
	if(products.indexOf("|") == -1) {
		productList=products.replace(/,;/g, ",;s|na|").replace(/&quot;/g, '\"').replace(/&amp;/g, '\&').replace(/&apos;/g, '\'');
        s.products =";s|na|" + productList;
	}
	else {
		productList=products.replace(/,;/g, ",;s|").replace(/&quot;/g, '\"').replace(/&amp;/g, '\&').replace(/&apos;/g, '\'');
		s.products =";s|" + productList;
    }
    s.products += ",;c|" + componentName;
    s.products += "|" + componentTitle;
    s.products += "|" + imageCount;
    s.products += "|" + productCount;
    s.products += "|" + visibleProductCount;
    s.products += "|" + perImageProductCount;
    s.products += "|" + productPosition;
	s.products=s.products.toLowerCase();
    // set relevant context data    
	s.contextData["shoppingProducts"] = "D=products";
	s.contextData["partner"] = partner;	
	// mention all variables to track
	var contextVars = ['shopping','componentName','componentTitle','partner','products','imageCount','productCount','visibleProductCount','perImageProductCount','productPosition','eventType'];
    s.linkTrackVars = 'products,contextData.shoppingProducts';
    s.linkTrackVars += ',contextData.' + contextVars.join(',contextData.');
    
    // send click beacons
	s.events=null; // make sure this has been cleared
	if(eventType == "impression") {
        // Additional variables set to track custom event
        s.linkTrackVars += ",contextData.eventShoppingProductsImpressions";
        s.contextData["eventShoppingProductsImpressions"] = "1";
        // track prodView, out-of-box event
        s.linkTrackEvents = "prodView";
        s.events = "prodView";
        
		s.tl(this,"o","shopping - products impression");
	}
	else if(eventType == "click") {
        // track scAdd, out-of-box event
		s.linkTrackEvents = "scAdd";
        s.events = "scAdd";        
		s.tl(this,"o","shopping - product click");
        console.log('2021-14-04 shoptrack function fired');
	}
    
    // Clear some of these products-specific variables
	while ( contextVars.length > 0 ) {
		s.contextData[contextVars.pop()] = "";
	}
	s.events="";
	s.products="";
	s.contextData["shoppingProducts"]="";
	s.contextData["partner"]="";
	
    // Probably meant to make sure it doesn't run twice
	sessionStorage.setItem("prodSetByShopTrack", "false");
}

var linkTitle = function($element, $cardConfig) {
    var wsRegex = /\s+/g;
    var innerText;
    var cardType = $cardConfig.cardType ? $cardConfig.cardType + "|" : "|";
    var hasImg = $element.has('img').length;
    if ($element[0].hasAttribute('title')) {
        var result = '';
        if (hasImg) {
          result += 'IMG|'
        } else {
          result += 'TXT|'
        }
        result += cardType;
        result += $element.attr('title').trim().replace(wsRegex, ' ');
        return result;
    }
    if ($element.is('[data-launch-selector]')) {
      return 'TXT|' + cardType + $element
            .find('[class*=a-HeadlineText]')
            .first()
            .text()
            .trim()
            .replace(wsRegex, ' ')
    }

            .closest('[class*=m-MediaWrap]', '.parbase')
            .siblings('[class*=m-TextWrap]')

            .replace(wsRegex, ' ');
    }
    innerText = $element.first().text().trim().replace(wsRegex, ' ');
    if (innerText.length) {
        return 'TXT|'+ cardType + innerText;
    }
}

var clickTrack = function($element) {
    var $tracker = $element.parents().siblings(".clicktracking").first();
    var $module = $tracker.parent();
    var moduleName = $tracker.attr('data-resource-type').split('/').pop();
    var moduleIndex = $('.clicktracking').index($tracker)
    var linkIndex = $module.find(clickSelector).index($element)

  var componentPayload, $componentConfig = {'componentTitle':''};
    try {
        //var componentConfig = JSON.parse($module.find('[data-analytics-config]').text());
        componentPayload = $module.find('[data-analytics-config]').text();
        if (componentPayload) {
            $componentConfig = JSON.parse(componentPayload);
        }
    } catch (err) {
        $componentConfig = {'componentTitle':''};
    }
    try {
        cardPayload = $element.closest('[data-analytics]', $module).attr('data-analytics');
        if (cardPayload) {
            $cardConfig = JSON.parse(cardPayload);
        }
    } catch (err) {
      cardConfig = {'cardType':''};
    }
    return Object.assign({}, {
        ModuleName: moduleName,
        ModuleIndex: moduleIndex,
        LinkTitle: linkTitle($element,  $cardConfig),
        LocUrl: window.location.href,
        LinkPosition: linkIndex,
        TargetUrl: $element.attr('href'),
        ComponentTitle: $componentConfig.componentTitle
        });//, componentConfig, cardConfig);
}
